function ck_sess_connect()
{
$.ajax({
url: 'ck_sess_connect.php',
data: {
},
type : 'POST',
timeout: 30000,
success: function(txt){
if (txt=='1'){
return true;
}else{
location.replace(window.location.href.replace('#',''));
}
},
error: function(){
location.replace(window.location.href.replace('#',''));
}
});
}

function cancella_firma(){
var conf=false;
if( $("#firmaparziale").is(':checked') == true){
// al momento non faccio niente
conf=confirm("Vuoi aggiungere una firma?");
}
else{

conf=false;
alert("Non è possibile sovrascrivere un'ora firmata");



}
return conf;
};
function check_classe_id(){
return !('1095223'.length == 0  );
}


var el_clicked = null;
$(document).ready( function() {

if(autoFirma == '1')
{
$('#open_firma').click();
}

$('.mie_lezioni').click( function() {
box_item='';
$.each(materie_classe, function() {
if (mygruppo ==1){
box_item = box_item + "<p class='rigtab' style='padding:5px;'><a style='color:red;' href='gioprof.php?gruppo_id="+this.classe_desc+"&materia="+this.materia_id+"&ope=LEZ&codocenza=1'>"+this.materia_desc+"</a></p>";
}else{
box_item = box_item + "<p class='rigtab' style='padding:5px;'><a style='color:red;' href='gioprof.php?classe_id="+this.classe_ident+"&materia="+this.materia_id+"&ope=LEZ&codocenza=1'>"+this.materia_desc+"</a></p>";
}

//alert(this.id)
});
$( "<div>"+box_item+"</div>" )
.clone()
.css('overflow','visible')
.appendTo('body')
.dialog({
title: "Selezionare una materia",
modal:true,
width: 550,
close: function(){$(this).remove();},
buttons: {
Chiudi: function() {
$(this).dialog("close");
}
}
})
})

$('#lampeggio.nonletto').effect("pulsate", { times:6 }, 1500);

$('#cambiadata').datepicker(
{
defaultDate: V_default_date,

$('#cambiadata').datepicker('destroy');

},
onChangeMonthYear: function()
{
setTimeout(function()
{
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="selectDay"]').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="selectDay"]').attr('tab_item_for', "this");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="selectDay"]').each(function()
{
$(this).attr('aria-label', $(this).text()+'/'+(parseInt($(this).attr('data-month'))+1)+'/'+$(this).attr('data-year'));
});
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="prev"]').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="prev"]').attr('aria-label', "Vai al mese precedente");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="prev"]').attr('tab_item_for', "this");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('aria-label', "Vai al mese successivo");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('tab_item_for', "this");
}, 100);
}
}
);
$('#cambiadata').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata').attr('aria-label', "Popup di selezione data");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="selectDay"]').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="selectDay"]').attr('tab_item_for', "this");

{

});

$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('tabindex', "2");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('aria-label', "Vai al mese successivo");
$('#cambiadata [data-handler="next"]').attr('tab_item_for', "this");
});
$.datepicker.setDefaults(
$.extend(
{
showMonthAfterYear: false
},
$.datepicker.regional[locale]
)
);

$('#scritta_tim').click( function() {
if($(this).attr('stato') == 'P'){
$(this).attr('stato','M');
$("#scritta_tim").html("mostra stato");
$(".tim_desc_mensa").show();
$(".tim_desc_stato").hide();
}
else{
$(this).attr('stato','P');
$("#scritta_tim").html("mostra mensa");
$(".tim_desc_mensa").hide();
$(".tim_desc_stato").show();
}

})

$(document).keydown(function(e)
{
var el = document.activeElement;

if(el.hasAttribute('tab_item_for') && (e.which == 13 || (e.which == 32 && !$(el).is("input") && !$(el).is("textarea"))))
{
if(el.tagName !== 'SELECT')
{
e.preventDefault();
e.stopPropagation();
}

var event_el = ($(el).attr('tab_item_for') == 'this') ? el : $(el).attr('tab_item_for');

$(event_el).focus();
$(event_el).click();
}
});

});
